 (* Write a  function to count true booleans in the given list. *)
let count_trues x =
  let rec count_trues_aux x =
    match x with
    | [] -> 0
    | x :: xs ->
        if x then count_trues_aux xs else count_trues_aux xs
  in
  count_trues_aux x

  let y = count_trues xs in
